To Change The Font Size

  • In Firefox, Internet Explorer and Netscape hold 'Ctrl' and press '+' or '-' to change the size of the text. Further instructions are available for Internet Explorer.
  • In Safari users need to hold the 'Apple' key and press '+' or '-' in order to change the size of the text.
  • In Opera press '+' or '-' to change the size of the text.
